### [165] [GelSLAM: A Real-time, High-Fidelity, and Robust 3D Tactile SLAM System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15990)
*Hung-Jui Huang,Mohammad Amin Mirzaee,Michael Kaess,Wenzhen Yuan*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: GelSLAM是一种实时的3D SLAM系统，它仅依靠触觉传感来长时间估计物体姿态并高精度重建物体形状。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确抓取和操作需要准确感知物体的姿态和形状。与视觉方法相比，触觉传感在接触中跟踪和重建物体时，具有更高的精度和不受遮挡影响的优势，这对于手内和高精度操作任务特别有价值。

Method: GelSLAM系统完全依赖触觉传感，利用触觉派生的表面法线和曲率进行鲁棒的跟踪和闭环检测，而非传统的点云方法。它能够实时估计物体姿态并重建其形状。

Result: GelSLAM能够实时跟踪物体运动，具有低误差和最小漂移。即使对于低纹理物体（如木制工具），也能实现亚毫米级的形状重建精度。它将触觉传感从局部接触扩展到全局、长距离的空间感知。

Conclusion: GelSLAM为许多涉及手内物体交互的精确操作任务奠定了基础，将触觉传感能力提升到全局、长距离的空间感知水平。

Abstract: Accurately perceiving an object's pose and shape is essential for precise
grasping and manipulation. Compared to common vision-based methods, tactile
sensing offers advantages in precision and immunity to occlusion when tracking
and reconstructing objects in contact. This makes it particularly valuable for
in-hand and other high-precision manipulation tasks. In this work, we present
GelSLAM, a real-time 3D SLAM system that relies solely on tactile sensing to
estimate object pose over long periods and reconstruct object shapes with high
fidelity. Unlike traditional point cloud-based approaches, GelSLAM uses
tactile-derived surface normals and curvatures for robust tracking and loop
closure. It can track object motion in real time with low error and minimal
drift, and reconstruct shapes with submillimeter accuracy, even for low-texture
objects such as wooden tools. GelSLAM extends tactile sensing beyond local
contact to enable global, long-horizon spatial perception, and we believe it
will serve as a foundation for many precise manipulation tasks involving
interaction with objects in hand. The video demo is available on our website:
https://joehjhuang.github.io/gelslam.

</details>

### [167] [Take That for Me: Multimodal Exophora Resolution with Interactive Questioning for Ambiguous Out-of-View Instructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16143)
*Akira Oyama,Shoichi Hasegawa,Akira Taniguchi,Yoshinobu Hagiwara,Tadahiro Taniguchi*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出MIEL框架，通过结合声源定位（SSL）、语义地图、视觉语言模型（VLM）和基于GPT-4o的交互式提问，解决了日常服务机器人解释涉及指示词的模糊指令（外指代）的挑战，尤其是在物体或用户不在机器人视野内的情况下。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 日常生活中，服务机器人需要理解包含“那个杯子”等指示词的模糊口头指令，即使物体或用户不在视野中。现有的外指代解析方法主要依赖视觉数据，因此在物体或用户不可见的真实世界场景中会失效。

Method: MIEL（Multimodal Interactive Exophora resolution with user Localization）框架整合了声源定位（SSL）、语义建图、视觉语言模型（VLM）和与GPT-4o的交互式提问。该方法首先构建环境的语义地图，并结合用户骨骼数据从语言查询中估计候选对象。SSL用于将机器人转向初始不在其视野内的用户，从而准确识别用户手势和指向方向。当仍存在歧义时，机器人会主动与用户互动，利用GPT-4o生成澄清性问题。

Result: 在真实世界环境中的实验表明，与不使用SSL和交互式提问的方法相比，当用户可见时，MIEL的结果约好1.3倍；当用户不可见时，结果约好2.0倍。

Conclusion: MIEL框架通过结合多模态感知（尤其是声源定位）和基于大型语言模型的交互式澄清，显著提高了外指代解析的准确性，特别是在用户或目标对象不在机器人视野范围内的复杂场景中。

Abstract: Daily life support robots must interpret ambiguous verbal instructions
involving demonstratives such as ``Bring me that cup,'' even when objects or
users are out of the robot's view. Existing approaches to exophora resolution
primarily rely on visual data and thus fail in real-world scenarios where the
object or user is not visible. We propose Multimodal Interactive Exophora
resolution with user Localization (MIEL), which is a multimodal exophora
resolution framework leveraging sound source localization (SSL), semantic
mapping, visual-language models (VLMs), and interactive questioning with
GPT-4o. Our approach first constructs a semantic map of the environment and
estimates candidate objects from a linguistic query with the user's skeletal
data. SSL is utilized to orient the robot toward users who are initially
outside its visual field, enabling accurate identification of user gestures and
pointing directions. When ambiguities remain, the robot proactively interacts
with the user, employing GPT-4o to formulate clarifying questions. Experiments
in a real-world environment showed results that were approximately 1.3 times
better when the user was visible to the robot and 2.0 times better when the
user was not visible to the robot, compared to the methods without SSL and
interactive questioning. The project website is
https://emergentsystemlabstudent.github.io/MIEL/.

Method: 该方法采用基于高斯过程的轮廓表示来建模每个对象，并通过递归方案在线更新这些轮廓以实现高效内存使用。SLAM问题在完全贝叶斯框架下构建，允许对机器人位姿和基于对象的地图进行联合推断，并支持概率性的测量到对象关联。

Abstract: We present a novel Simultaneous Localization and Mapping (SLAM) method that

on a per object basis using GP based contour representations. These contours
are updated online through a recursive scheme, enabling efficient memory usage.
The SLAM problem is formulated within a fully Bayesian framework, allowing
joint inference over the robot pose and object based map. This representation
provides semantic information such as the number of objects and their areas,
while also supporting probabilistic measurement to object associations.
Furthermore, the GP based contours yield confidence bounds on object shapes,
offering valuable information for downstream tasks like safe navigation and
exploration. We validate our method on synthetic and real world experiments,
and show that it delivers accurate localization and mapping performance across
diverse structured environments.

### [169] [Swarming Without an Anchor (SWA): Robot Swarms Adapt Better to Localization Dropouts Then a Single Robot](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16460)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在无人机群中，个体定位（ego-localization）可能出现间歇性故障或不可用，导致难以维持准确的态势感知和群体凝聚力。因此，需要一种鲁棒的方法来应对这种挑战，提高多无人机系统的可靠性和弹性。

Method: SWA方法融合了去中心化状态估计、鲁棒的相互感知和机载传感器数据。它利用相对信息来估计无人机的横向状态，并识别相对于局部星座的明确状态。该任务被视为双积分器同步问题，以实现速度共识。该方法通过仿真和实际实验进行验证。

Result: 该方法能够衰减除整个群体均匀平移漂移之外的所有干扰和性能下降。它成功地在主要定位不可靠或不可用的挑战性条件下，维持了无人机群的内聚行为。这为利用紧密协作提高多无人机系统的可靠性和弹性提供了新机会。

Abstract: In this paper, we present the Swarming Without an Anchor (SWA) approach to
state estimation in swarms of Unmanned Aerial Vehicles (UAVs) experiencing
ego-localization dropout, where individual agents are laterally stabilized
using relative information only. We propose to fuse decentralized state
estimation with robust mutual perception and onboard sensor data to maintain
accurate state awareness despite intermittent localization failures. Thus, the
relative information used to estimate the lateral state of UAVs enables the
identification of the unambiguous state of UAVs with respect to the local
constellation. The resulting behavior reaches velocity consensus, as this task
can be referred to as the double integrator synchronization problem. All
disturbances and performance degradations except a uniform translation drift of
the swarm as a whole is attenuated which is enabling new opportunities in using
tight cooperation for increasing reliability and resilience of multi-UAV
systems. Simulations and real-world experiments validate the effectiveness of
our approach, demonstrating its capability to sustain cohesive swarm behavior
in challenging conditions of unreliable or unavailable primary localization.

Method: 该研究开发了一个针对波士顿动力Spot机器人的地形分类器。它利用Spot提供的100多个本体感知信号（如足部穿透、力、关节角度等），首先应用降维技术从信号中提取相关信息，然后采用分类技术根据可通行性区分地形类型。

to create a traversability map to plan safer paths for the robot to navigate.
The work presented here is a terrain classifier developed for a Boston Dynamics

### [171] [On Kinodynamic Global Planning in a Simplicial Complex Environment: A Mixed Integer Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16511)
*Otobong Jerome,Alexandr Klimchik,Alexander Maloletov,Geesara Kulathunga*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该研究将类汽车的运动学规划问题转化为优化任务，以计算满足速度、加速度和转向边界条件的最短时间轨迹，并通过混合整数线性规划方法实现高效求解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法在处理类汽车的运动学规划问题时，难以同时优化空间路径和控制序列，并在复杂的3D环境中避免局部最优，同时确保严格遵守约束并实现最短时间。

Method: 该方法将运动学规划问题建模为优化任务，同时优化空间路径和加速度/转向控制序列。它最初是一个带二次约束的混合整数分数规划，通过变量变换重构为混合整数双线性目标，然后利用McCormick包络松弛为混合整数线性规划（MILP），以避免局部最小值并在单纯形复形环境中高效运行。

Result: 与MPPI和log-MPPI等现有规划器相比，该方法生成解决方案的速度快104倍，并且严格遵守所有指定约束。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种高效且严格遵守约束的类汽车运动学规划方法，通过创新的优化框架，显著提高了计算速度，并能够处理复杂的环境和运动限制。

Abstract: This work casts the kinodynamic planning problem for car-like vehicles as an
optimization task to compute a minimum-time trajectory and its associated
velocity profile, subject to boundary conditions on velocity, acceleration, and
steering. The approach simultaneously optimizes both the spatial path and the
sequence of acceleration and steering controls, ensuring continuous motion from
a specified initial position and velocity to a target end position and
velocity.The method analyzes the admissible control space and terrain to avoid
local minima. The proposed method operates efficiently in simplicial complex
environments, a preferred terrain representation for capturing intricate 3D
landscapes. The problem is initially posed as a mixed-integer fractional
program with quadratic constraints, which is then reformulated into a
mixed-integer bilinear objective through a variable transformation and
subsequently relaxed to a mixed-integer linear program using McCormick
envelopes. Comparative simulations against planners such as MPPI and log-MPPI
demonstrate that the proposed approach generates solutions 104 times faster
while strictly adhering to the specified constraints

### [172] [Comparative Analysis of UAV Path Planning Algorithms for Efficient Navigation in Urban 3D Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16515)
*Hichem Cheriet,Khellat Kihel Badra,Chouraqui Samira*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文通过在3D城市环境中进行实验，比较了A*、RRT*和粒子群优化（PSO）三种无人机路径规划算法的有效性和效率。结果显示A*在计算效率和路径质量上表现最佳，PSO适合密集环境和急转弯，而RRT*则提供了良好的平衡性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无人机（UAV）路径规划和避障是关键挑战。尽管现有路径规划算法已成功解决问题，但它们仍面临多重挑战和局限性。因此，需要对广泛使用的算法进行评估，以测试它们的有效性和效率。

Method: 本文在模拟的3D城市环境中进行了广泛实验，该环境模拟了充满障碍物的城市。设计了三个实验，每个包含两个场景，以测试A*、RRT*和粒子群优化（PSO）这三种常用算法。实验考虑了不同的城市地图大小、不同的飞行高度以及环境中变化的障碍物密度和尺寸。

Result: 实验结果表明，A*算法在计算效率和路径质量方面均优于其他算法。粒子群优化（PSO）算法特别适用于急转弯和密集环境。RR*算法由于其随机寻优方法，在所有实验中都表现出良好的平衡性并运行良好。

Conclusion: A*算法在综合性能（计算效率和路径质量）上表现最佳，PSO算法在特定复杂（急转弯和密集）环境中具有优势，而RRT*算法则提供了一种稳健且平衡的通用解决方案。这些发现为无人机在不同城市环境下的路径规划算法选择提供了实证依据。

Abstract: The most crucial challenges for UAVs are planning paths and avoiding
obstacles in their way. In recent years, a wide variety of path-planning
algorithms have been developed. These algorithms have successfully solved
path-planning problems; however, they suffer from multiple challenges and
limitations. To test the effectiveness and efficiency of three widely used
algorithms, namely A*, RRT*, and Particle Swarm Optimization (PSO), this paper
conducts extensive experiments in 3D urban city environments cluttered with
obstacles. Three experiments were designed with two scenarios each to test the
aforementioned algorithms. These experiments consider different city map sizes,
different altitudes, and varying obstacle densities and sizes in the
environment. According to the experimental results, the A* algorithm
outperforms the others in both computation efficiency and path quality. PSO is
especially suitable for tight turns and dense environments, and RRT* offers a
balance and works well across all experiments due to its randomized approach to
finding solutions.

</details>

### [174] [Observer-Free Sliding Mode Control via Structured Decomposition: a Smooth and Bounded Control Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15787)
*Jaafar Gaber*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的滑模控制方法通常需要状态观测器和高阶导数，并可能导致抖振。本研究旨在解决这些问题，提供一种更实用、高效的替代方案。

Abstract: In this paper, we introduce an observer-free sliding mode control (SMC)

observers and higher-order derivatives, reduces chattering, and yields smooth,
bounded control signal. Simulation results confirms its robustness and
stability on benchmark nonlinear systems (pendulum, Van der Pol, Duffing, and

scalable and practical alternative to traditional SMC, well suited for embedded
and distributed environments.

increase in driving range or overall cost savings by reducing battery capacity
while maintaining the same range. Harmonic motor losses account for an
avoidable share of more than 30% of the total eDrive losses in standard B6-2L
300 kW iPMSM configurations. These losses result from high-frequency voltage

approaches to loss reduction that have been developed by research and industry
in recent years. In particular, novel part-load-capable motor and inverter
concepts are introduced, which enable motor switching or multilevel operation
to reduce harmonic losses in the part-load range.

### [176] [Solving Three-phase AC Infeasibility Analysis to Near-zero Optimality Gap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15937)
*Bikram Panthee,Amritanshu Pandey*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种改进的三相不可行性分析（TPIA）方法，通过将非凸问题重新表述为精确的双线性规划，并结合空间分支定界算法和序贯边界收紧技术，实现了对大型配电网中弱点的全局最优识别，显著提高了计算效率和精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有三相不可行性分析（TPIA）问题是非凸的，可能存在局部最优解和鞍点，导致电网升级方案次优。因此，需要一种能够找到全局最优解的方法来准确识别电网中的弱点。

Method: 作者将原始的非凸非线性规划（NLP）问题重新表述为一个精确的非凸双线性规划（BLP）。随后，应用空间分支定界（SBnB）算法来计算接近零最优性间隙的解。为提高SBnB性能，引入了一种带有变量过滤和分解的边界收紧算法，称为序贯边界收紧（SBT），以收紧双线性变量的边界。

Result: 所提出的方法能够解决节点数超过5000的大规模三相不可行性分析问题，并实现小于10e-4的最优性间隙。序贯边界收紧（SBT）显著提高了Gurobi的SBnB算法的效率和准确性。此外，通过使用开发的预求解例程进行边界处理，可以将SBnB的运行时间缩短高达97%。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一种高效、精确的全局优化方法，能够解决大规模三相不可行性分析问题，并识别配电网中的最优弱点。通过双线性规划重构和改进的边界收紧技术，显著提升了算法的性能和实用性。

Abstract: Recent works have shown the use of equivalent circuit-based infeasibility
analysis to identify weak locations in distribution power grids. For
three-phase power flow problems, when the power flow solver diverges,
three-phase infeasibility analysis (TPIA) can converge and identify weak
locations. The original TPIA problem is non-convex, and local minima and saddle
points are possible. This can result in grid upgrades that are sub-optimal. To
address this issue, we reformulate the original non-convex nonlinear program
(NLP) as an exact non-convex bilinear program (BLP). Subsequently, we apply the
spatial branch-and-bound (SBnB) algorithm to compute a solution with near-zero
optimality gap. To improve SBnB performance, we introduce a bound tightening
algorithm with variable filtering and decomposition, which tightens bounds on
bilinear variables. We demonstrate that sequential bound tightening (SBT)
significantly improves the efficiency and accuracy of Gurobi's SBnB algorithm.
Our results show that the proposed method can solve large-scale three-phase
infeasibility analysis problems with >5k nodes, achieving an optimality gap of
less than 10e-4. Furthermore, we demonstrate that by utilizing the developed
presolve routine for bounding, we can reduce the runtime of SBnB by up to 97%.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将无人机整合到卡车配送系统可提高可达性、降低成本和提高效率，但无人机部署会产生采购、维护和能源消耗等成本。其效益取决于服务需求，在低需求区域可能导致资源利用不足。此外，由于不可预见的事件或基础设施中断，准确预测需求具有挑战性。

Method: 采用市场进入和退出实物期权方法，在随机需求下优化卡车专用和无人机辅助配送之间的切换。进一步开发了随机多选项模型，以动态切换不同数量无人机的配送模式。将这些模型应用于迈阿密-戴德县，评估了三家主要物流运营商的动态切换成本。

Result: 在高需求区域，每辆卡车部署多架无人机能带来显著的成本优势。与即时节约成本的切换相比，所提出的动态切换模型（确定性和随机性）分别将成本降低了17.4%和31.3%。敏感性分析显示，随机参数对进入和退出时机具有不对称影响。在迈阿密-戴德县，评估了主要物流运营商的动态切换成本。

Conclusion: 本研究强调了动态配送切换的潜在益处，并为优化物流运营提供了重要见解，尤其是在处理随机需求和无人机部署方面。

Abstract: Integrating drones into truck delivery systems can improve customer
accessibility, reduce operational costs, and increase delivery efficiency.
However, drone deployment incurs costs, including procurement, maintenance, and
energy consumption, and its benefits depend on service demand. In low-demand
areas, drone-assisted trucks may underutilize resources due to high upfront
costs. Accurately predicting demand is challenging due to uncertainties from
unforeseen events or infrastructure disruptions. To address this, a market
entry and exit real option approach is used to optimize switching between
truck-only and drone-assisted delivery under stochastic demand. Results show
that deploying multiple drones per truck offers significant cost advantages in
high-demand regions. Using the proposed dynamic switching model, deterministic
and stochastic approaches reduce costs by 17.4% and 31.3%, respectively,
compared to immediate cost-saving switching. Sensitivity analysis reveals
asymmetric effects of stochastic parameters on entry and exit timings. A
stochastic multiple-options model is further developed to dynamically switch
between truck-only and drone-assisted delivery with varying drone numbers.
Applying these models to Miami-Dade County, we evaluate dynamic switching costs
for three major logistics operators. This study highlights the potential
benefits of dynamic delivery switching and provides insights for optimizing
logistics operations.

### [178] [Data-Driven Analysis and Predictive Control of Descriptor Systems with Application to Power and Water Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16091)
*Yuan Zhang,Yu Wang,Jun Shang,Jinhui Zhang*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文为离散时间描述符系统开发了一个全面的数据驱动分析与控制框架，解决了非因果性问题，并扩展了数据使能预测控制（DeePC）以处理不完全可控系统，并在电力和水网络案例中展示了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管数据驱动分析和控制受到广泛关注，但对于描述符系统（对建模具有代数约束的复杂工程系统至关重要，如电力和水网络）的研究相对较少。此外，处理描述符系统中的非因果性是一个基本挑战。

Method: 通过构建前向和后向数据矩阵来处理非因果性；建立了基于输入输出数据的可控性（R-可控性、C-可控性）和可观测性（R-可观测性、C-可观测性）的充分条件；将Willems基本引理扩展到不完全可控系统；并应用数据使能预测控制（DeePC）实现描述符系统的输出跟踪。

Result: DeePC成功实现了描述符系统的输出跟踪，即使在不完全可控条件下也能保持性能。在IEEE 9总线电力系统中，DeePC在故意违反R-可控性时仍保持了频率稳定性；在EPANET水网络中，成功在代数约束下实现了压头控制的输出跟踪。

Conclusion: 本文为离散时间描述符系统提供了一个无需显式状态空间模型的全面数据驱动框架，通过解决非因果性和扩展对不完全可控系统的处理，显著提升了数据驱动控制在复杂工程系统中的应用能力。

Abstract: Despite growing interest in data-driven analysis and control of linear
systems, descriptor systems--which are essential for modeling complex
engineered systems with algebraic constraints like power and water
networks--have received comparatively little attention. This paper develops a
comprehensive data-driven framework for analyzing and controlling discrete-time
descriptor systems without relying on explicit state-space models. We address
fundamental challenges posed by non-causality through the construction of
forward and backward data matrices, establishing data-based sufficient
conditions for controllability and observability in terms of input-output data,
where both R-controllability and C-controllability (R-observability and
C-observability) have been considered. We then extend Willems' fundamental
lemma to incompletely controllable systems. These methodological advances
enable Data-Enabled Predictive Control (DeePC) to achieve output tracking in
descriptor systems and to maintain performance under incomplete controllability
conditions, as demonstrated in two case studies: i) Frequency regulation in an
IEEE 9-bus power system with 3 generators, where DeePC maintained the frequency
stability of the power system despite deliberate violations of
R-controllability; and ii) Pressure head control in an EPANET water network
with 3 tanks, 2 reservoirs, and 117 pipes, where output tracking was
successfully enforced under algebraic constraints.

*Yuhao Zheng,Ting You,Kejia Peng,Chang Liu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在卫星-地面边缘计算网络中，需要解决安全任务调度固有的复杂性，并同时平衡传输延迟、能量消耗和物理层安全等多个目标。

Method: 本文提出一个两阶段优化框架：第一阶段设计了保密感知的用户关联策略，通过离散化人工噪声功率比并识别满足保密约束的可行链路，生成候选安全关联；第二阶段将延迟-能量感知的任务调度问题建模为整数线性规划，并使用启发式蜉蝣算法（MA）求解以获得低复杂度、高质量的解决方案。

Result: 广泛的仿真结果表明，所提出的框架在动态卫星环境下实现了安全高效的任务调度，并展示了其有效性和优越性。

Conclusion: 所提出的两阶段优化框架能够有效且优越地解决卫星-地面边缘计算网络中的安全任务调度问题，成功平衡了传输延迟、能耗和物理层安全。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a two-stage optimization framework for secure task
scheduling in satellite-terrestrial edge computing networks (STECNs). The
framework jointly considers secure user association and task offloading to
balance transmission delay, energy consumption, and physical-layer security. To
address the inherent complexity, we decouple the problem into two stages. In
the first stage, a secrecy-aware user association strategy is designed by
discretizing artificial noise (AN) power ratios and identifying feasible links
that satisfy secrecy constraints, resulting in a set of candidate secure
associations. In the second stage, we formulate a delay-energy-aware task
scheduling problem as an integer linear program and solve it using a heuristic
Mayfly Algorithm (MA) to obtain low-complexity, high-quality solutions.
Extensive simulation results demonstrate the effectiveness and superiority of
the proposed framework in achieving secure and efficient task scheduling under
dynamic satellite environments.

### [180] [Resilient Control for Networked Switched Systems With/Without ACK: An Active Quantized Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16296)
*Rui Zhao,Zhiqiang Zuo,Yijing Wang,Wentao Zhang,Yang Shi*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文研究了拒绝服务（DoS）攻击下切换系统的量化控制问题，提出了四种结合不同控制器、量化器和网络配置的控制策略，旨在实现渐近稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在DoS攻击下，如何对切换系统进行量化控制是一个挑战。研究动机在于考虑系统的防御能力以及量化器和控制器的计算资源限制，设计有效的控制策略以确保系统稳定性。

Method: 本文提出了四种控制策略，结合了主动/被动控制器、以原点为中心/定制设计的量化器以及带/不带ACK信号的网络配置。具体方法包括：为编码器和解码器设计避免量化饱和的更新律；通过传输额外信息保持编码器和解码器操作的一致性；考虑异步行为，推导出关于切换信号和DoS攻击约束的渐近稳定性充分条件；提出主动量化策略（带ACK信号），利用系统模型信息实时计算控制信号；开发被动量化策略（带ACK信号）作为简化版；受时间触发和事件触发机制启发，研究不带ACK信号的被动量化策略，并提供两种可行的量化器更新律。

Result: 研究结果表明，所提出的策略能够实现系统状态的渐近稳定性，即使在DoS攻击下也能实现可能的收敛。特别是，带ACK信号的主动量化策略能够利用系统模型信息实时计算控制信号，从而减轻DoS攻击的影响。通过精心设计的切换信号可以进一步缓解DoS攻击。两种仿真验证了所提策略的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的四种量化控制策略，通过不同的配置组合，有效解决了DoS攻击下切换系统的控制问题，能够实现系统的渐近稳定性，并通过仿真验证了其有效性。

Abstract: This paper deals with the quantized control problem for switched systems
under denial-of-service (DoS) attack.
  Considering the system's defensive capability and the computational resources
of quantizers and controllers, four control strategies are proposed. These
strategies incorporate different combinations of controllers (active and
passive), quantizers (centered on the origin or custom-designed), and network
configurations (with or without ACK signals). For each strategy, specific
update laws for the encoder and decoder are designed to avoid quantization
saturation.
  Furthermore, the uniformity of encoder and decoder operations is maintained
by transmitting additional information to the decoder. To achieve asymptotic
stability, sufficient conditions concerning the switching signal and DoS attack
constraints are derived by taking into account the asynchronous behaviors. The
proposed active quantization strategy with the ACK signal leverages the system
model information to compute the control signal in real-time, allowing for
possible convergence of the system state despite DoS attack. Additionally, a
well-designed switching signal is suggested to further mitigate the impact of
DoS attack. A passive quantization strategy with ACK signal is also developed
as a simplified version of the active quantized control strategy, providing the
foundation for a strategy without ACK signal. Inspired by time-triggered and
event-triggered mechanisms, the passive quantization strategy without ACK
signal is investigated, with two feasible update laws for the quantizer.
Finally, two simulations are conducted to validate the effectiveness of the
proposed strategies.

### [181] [Performance analysis for cone-preserving switched systems with constrained switching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16450)
*Marc Seidel,Richard Pates,Frank Allgöwer*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究更一般的锥保持线性离散时间切换系统，以推广现有切换系统和正切换系统的性能与稳定性分析结果，提供统一的视角，并为受限切换的正切换系统提供新的$\ell_1$-性能分析条件。

Method: 研究由自动机控制切换的锥保持线性离散时间切换系统，提出性能分析条件，并利用锥保持视角为Lyapunov函数选择提供见解。

Result: 提出了适用于广泛性能度量的性能分析条件；统一并推广了切换系统和正切换系统性能与稳定性分析的已知结果；为受限切换的正切换系统提供了新颖的$\ell_1$-性能分析条件；锥保持视角为Lyapunov函数的选择提供了见解。

Conclusion: 本文为锥保持线性离散时间切换系统提供了一个统一的性能分析框架，推广了现有结果，并提出了新的$\ell_1$-性能分析条件，对Lyapunov函数选择提供了实用指导。

Abstract: This paper studies cone-preserving linear discrete-time switched systems
whose switching is governed by an automaton. For this general system class, we
present performance analysis conditions for a broadly usable performance
measure. In doing so, we generalize several known results for performance and
stability analysis for switched and positive switched systems, providing a
unifying perspective. We also arrive at novel $\ell_1$-performance analysis
conditions for positive switched systems with constrained switching, for which
we present an application-motivated numerical example. Further, the
cone-preserving perspective provides insights into appropriate Lyapunov
function selection.

### [182] [Wide-Area Power System Oscillations from Large-Scale AI Workloads](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16457)
*Min-Seung Ko,Hao Zhu*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的动态功率剖析方法，用于建模以AI为中心的数据中心负载，并分析其对电网运行的影响，特别是其诱发广域电网振荡的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模AI工作负载（训练和微调阶段）具有周期性随机功率波动，这与传统负载爬坡不同，可能作为持续强制输入与电网振内模式相互作用并放大振荡，因此需要研究其对电网的影响。

Method: 开发了一种动态功率剖析方法来表征AI负载的功率波动；使用WECC 179总线系统作为测试案例，模拟并检验了系统强度、渗透水平、波动频率范围、单个数据中心规模和地理部署等因素对振荡响应幅度和变异性的影响。

Result: 模拟结果显示，更窄的波动频带、更大的单站点容量或分散的选址会显著加剧多个模式的振荡。

Conclusion: 该研究的模型和数值分析为将AI主导的电力需求整合到电网振荡研究中提供了定量基础，并支持开发新的规划和运行措施，以应对AI负载的持续增长。

Abstract: This paper develops a new dynamic power profiling approach for modeling
AI-centric datacenter loads and analyzing their impact on grid operations,
particularly their potential to induce wide-area grid oscillations. We
characterize the periodic stochastic power fluctuations inherent to large-scale
AI workloads during both the training and fine-tuning stages, driven by the
state-of-the-art GPU computing architecture designs. These sustained, large
power fluctuations, unlike conventional load ramping, act as persistent forcing
inputs capable of interacting with and amplifying local and inter-area
oscillation modes. Using the WECC 179-bus system as a test case, we examine the
amplitude and variability of oscillatory responses under different factors,
ranging from system strength, penetration level, fluctuation frequency range,
individual datacenter size, to geographical deployment. Simulation results show
that, notably, narrower fluctuation bands, larger single-site capacities, or
dispersed siting can intensify oscillations across multiple modes. Our models
and numerical studies provide a quantitative basis for integrating AI-dominant
electricity demands into grid oscillation studies, and further support the
development of new planning and operational measures to power the continuous AI
load growth.

### [183] [Reinforcement Learning-based Control via Y-wise Affine Neural Networks (YANNs)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16474)
*Austin Braniff,Yuhe Tian*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Y-wise仿射神经网络（YANNs）的新型强化学习（RL）算法YANN-RL。该算法利用YANNs的可解释性，通过线性最优控制解初始化RL的actor和critic网络，并扩展其以学习非线性系统，在安全关键系统中表现出显著优于现有RL算法的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的强化学习算法在处理复杂非线性系统时，往往需要从零开始学习，缺乏初始的置信度，且难以保证安全性。本研究旨在通过利用YANNs的可解释性及其表示分段仿射函数的能力，将已知的线性最优控制解融入RL算法的初始化中，从而为RL提供一个强大的、具有置信度的起点，并使其能够逐步学习非线性系统的最优控制策略，尤其是在考虑安全约束的场景下。

Method: 该方法的核心是YANN-RL算法：1. 使用YANNs作为RL的actor和critic网络，YANNs能够精确表示分段仿射函数。2. YANN-actor通过离线计算得到的近似线性系统模型的多参数控制解进行初始化。3. YANN-critic初始化为线性系统的状态-动作值函数的显式形式，并将奖励函数作为最优控制问题（OCP）的目标。4. 注入额外的网络层以扩展YANNs来处理非线性表达式，并通过与真实复杂非线性系统在线交互进行训练。5. 实施连续策略改进，以确保线性OCP解作为RL策略性能的有效下界。

Result: YANN-RL算法在剪切摆和安全关键化学反应系统上进行了验证。结果表明，YANN-RL显著优于使用深度确定性策略梯度（DDPG）的现代RL算法，尤其是在考虑安全约束时表现出更优异的性能。

Conclusion: YANN-RL算法通过结合YANNs的可解释性、线性最优控制的初始置信度以及在线学习非线性系统的能力，提供了一种有效且安全的强化学习方法。它能够从一个可靠的线性最优控制解开始，逐步学习解决复杂的非线性最优控制问题，并在实际应用中，特别是在涉及安全约束的场景下，展现出超越现有RL算法的优越性。

Abstract: This work presents a novel reinforcement learning (RL) algorithm based on
Y-wise Affine Neural Networks (YANNs). YANNs provide an interpretable neural
network which can exactly represent known piecewise affine functions of
arbitrary input and output dimensions defined on any amount of polytopic
subdomains. One representative application of YANNs is to reformulate explicit
solutions of multi-parametric linear model predictive control. Built on this,
we propose the use of YANNs to initialize RL actor and critic networks, which
enables the resulting YANN-RL control algorithm to start with the confidence of
linear optimal control. The YANN-actor is initialized by representing the
multi-parametric control solutions obtained via offline computation using an
approximated linear system model. The YANN-critic represents the explicit form
of the state-action value function for the linear system and the reward
function as the objective in an optimal control problem (OCP). Additional
network layers are injected to extend YANNs for nonlinear expressions, which
can be trained online by directly interacting with the true complex nonlinear
system. In this way, both the policy and state-value functions exactly
represent a linear OCP initially and are able to eventually learn the solution
of a general nonlinear OCP. Continuous policy improvement is also implemented
to provide heuristic confidence that the linear OCP solution serves as an
effective lower bound to the performance of RL policy. The YANN-RL algorithm is
demonstrated on a clipped pendulum and a safety-critical chemical-reactive
system. Our results show that YANN-RL significantly outperforms the modern RL
algorithm using deep deterministic policy gradient, especially when considering
safety constraints.

</details>

*Shili Wu,Yancheng Zhu,Aniruddha Datta,Sean B. Andersson*

Abstract: We consider the problem of using multiple agents to harvest data from a
collection of sensor nodes (targets) scattered across a two-dimensional
environment. These targets transmit their data to the agents that move in the
space above them, and our goal is for the agents to collect data from the
targets as efficiently as possible while moving to their final destinations.
The agents are assumed to have a continuous control action, and we leverage
reinforcement learning, specifically Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) with
Lagrangian Penalty (LP), to identify highly effective solutions. Additionally,
we enhance the controller's robustness by incorporating regularization at each
state to smooth the learned policy. We conduct a series of simulations to
demonstrate our approach and validate its performance and robustness.

### [185] [Robust Residual Finite Scalar Quantization for Neural Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15860)
*Xiaoxu Zhu*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 针对神经压缩中有限标量量化（FSQ）的残差幅度衰减问题，本文提出了鲁棒残差有限标量量化（RFSQ）框架，通过可学习缩放因子和可逆层归一化解决了该问题，显著优于现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限标量量化（FSQ）在神经压缩中表现出简化训练和提高稳定性等优势，但在残差量化框架中存在“残差幅度衰减问题”，导致后续FSQ层接收信号逐渐减弱，严重限制了其有效性。

Method: 本文提出了鲁棒残差有限标量量化（RFSQ）框架，通过两种新颖的条件策略解决残差幅度衰减问题：可学习的缩放因子和可逆层归一化。

Result: 在ImageNet上的综合实验表明，RFSQ变体显著优于包括VQ-EMA、FSQ和LFQ在内的强基线，在感知损失方面实现了高达45%的改进，L1重建误差减少了28.7%。其中，所提出的层归一化策略在不同配置下表现出最稳定的一致性改进。

Conclusion: RFSQ被确立为一种优越的神经压缩量化方法，特别是在采用层归一化策略时，能够有效实现多阶段残差量化，同时保持FSQ的简洁性。

Abstract: Finite Scalar Quantization (FSQ) has emerged as a promising alternative to
Vector Quantization (VQ) in neural compression, offering simplified training
and improved stability. However, naive application of FSQ in residual
quantization frameworks suffers from the \textbf{residual magnitude decay
problem}, where subsequent FSQ layers receive progressively weaker signals,
severely limiting their effectiveness. We propose \textbf{Robust Residual
Finite Scalar Quantization (RFSQ)}, a general framework that addresses this
fundamental limitation through two novel conditioning strategies: learnable
scaling factors and invertible layer normalization. Our approach maintains the
simplicity of FSQ while enabling effective multi-stage residual quantization.
Comprehensive experiments on ImageNet demonstrate that RFSQ variants
significantly outperform strong baselines including VQ-EMA, FSQ, and LFQ,
achieving up to 45\% improvement in perceptual loss and 28.7\% reduction in L1
reconstruction error. The proposed LayerNorm strategy shows the most consistent
improvements across different configurations, establishing RFSQ as a superior
quantization method for neural compression.

respectively.
  Results: Homogeneous T_1, T_2 and proton density weighted images are obtained

acquisition are simultaneously resolved independently of the TSE factor.

Abstract: Understanding the dynamic organization and homeostasis of living tissues

ensuring biologically meaningful outputs suitable for in silico experimentation
and hypothesis testing. Evaluation across layers and biological replicates

and high structural similarity while maintaining efficient inference through
model optimization. This work establishes VT-DTSN as a feasible, high-fidelity

### [188] [Structure-Preserving Medical Image Generation from a Latent Graph Representation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15920)
*Kevin Arias,Edwin Vargas,Kumar Vijay Mishra,Antonio Ortega,Henry Arguello*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新颖的生成模型，通过学习医学图像的潜在图表示（LGR）和图卷积网络（GCN）来生成结构保留的合成X射线图像，以解决数据稀缺问题并提高下游任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 监督学习在数据丰富时效果显著，但在医学影像领域，由于数据获取成本高、图像特征复杂，数据稀缺限制了深度神经网络的潜力。现有数据增强技术和生成模型未能充分考虑X射线图像等医学影像的高度结构化性质，忽略了其固有的语义关系和解剖限制。

Method: 研究引入了一种新型生成模型，通过学习潜在图表示（LGR）来捕捉X射线图像的内在结构。该模型是端到端的，包含两部分：(i) 学习LGR，(ii) 利用图卷积网络（GCN）从LGR重建X射线图像。模型采用对抗训练来指导生成器和判别器学习LGR的分布。通过将生成的LGR映射到X射线图像，可以生成结构保留的合成图像。此外，该方法还评估了学习到的图表示在X射线图像分类和分割等其他任务中的有效性。

Result: 该方法能够生成结构保留的合成图像。数值实验表明，其在分类任务中性能提高了高达3%，在分割任务中提高了2%。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于LGR和GCN的生成模型能够有效生成结构保留的合成医学图像，成功解决了医学影像数据稀缺的挑战，并显著提升了X射线图像分类和分割等任务的性能。

Abstract: Supervised learning techniques have proven their efficacy in many
applications with abundant data. However, applying these methods to medical
imaging is challenging due to the scarcity of data, given the high acquisition
costs and intricate data characteristics of those images, thereby limiting the
full potential of deep neural networks. To address the lack of data,
augmentation techniques leverage geometry, color, and the synthesis ability of
generative models (GMs). Despite previous efforts, gaps in the generation
process limit the impact of data augmentation to improve understanding of
medical images, e.g., the highly structured nature of some domains, such as
X-ray images, is ignored. Current GMs rely solely on the network's capacity to
blindly synthesize augmentations that preserve semantic relationships of chest
X-ray images, such as anatomical restrictions, representative structures, or
structural similarities consistent across datasets. In this paper, we introduce
a novel GM that leverages the structural resemblance of medical images by
learning a latent graph representation (LGR). We design an end-to-end model to
learn (i) a LGR that captures the intrinsic structure of X-ray images and (ii)
a graph convolutional network (GCN) that reconstructs the X-ray image from the
LGR. We employ adversarial training to guide the generator and discriminator
models in learning the distribution of the learned LGR. Using the learned GCN,
our approach generates structure-preserving synthetic images by mapping
generated LGRs to X-ray. Additionally, we evaluate the learned graph
representation for other tasks, such as X-ray image classification and
segmentation. Numerical experiments demonstrate the efficacy of our approach,
increasing performance up to $3\%$ and $2\%$ for classification and
segmentation, respectively.

</details>


### [189] [Decoding MGMT Methylation: A Step Towards Precision Medicine in Glioblastoma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16424)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胶质母细胞瘤侵袭性强，难以治疗，MGMT基因甲基化状态是预测患者对替莫唑胺治疗反应的关键生物标志物。然而，由于胶质母细胞瘤的复杂性和异质性，使用非侵入性影像技术准确预测MGMT甲基化状态极具挑战性。

Method: 本研究引入了“用于MGMT甲基化状态预测的卷积自编码器（CAMP）”框架，该框架基于自适应稀疏惩罚，分为两个阶段：1) 通过定制的自编码器生成合成MRI切片，有效捕获和保留不同MRI模态下的复杂组织和肿瘤结构；2) 使用由自适应稀疏惩罚增强的卷积神经网络预测MGMT甲基化状态，该惩罚能动态调整以适应MR图像中对比度差异和肿瘤位置等数据变化。

Result: CAMP方法在MRI图像合成方面表现出色，能保留所有MRI模态下的脑组织、脂肪和个体肿瘤结构。在基准数据集上验证，CAMP实现了0.97的准确率、0.98的特异性和0.97的敏感性，显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: CAMP框架的成果证明了其在改善MRI数据解读方面的潜力，并有望为胶质母细胞瘤患者提供更个性化的治疗策略。

Abstract: Glioblastomas, constituting over 50% of malignant brain tumors, are highly
aggressive brain tumors that pose substantial treatment challenges due to their
rapid progression and resistance to standard therapies. The methylation status
of the O-6-Methylguanine-DNA Methyltransferase (MGMT) gene is a critical
biomarker for predicting patient response to treatment, particularly with the
alkylating agent temozolomide. However, accurately predicting MGMT methylation
status using non-invasive imaging techniques remains challenging due to the
complex and heterogeneous nature of glioblastomas, that includes, uneven
contrast, variability within lesions, and irregular enhancement patterns. This
study introduces the Convolutional Autoencoders for MGMT Methylation Status
Prediction (CAMP) framework, which is based on adaptive sparse penalties to
enhance predictive accuracy. The CAMP framework operates in two phases: first,
generating synthetic MRI slices through a tailored autoencoder that effectively
captures and preserves intricate tissue and tumor structures across different
MRI modalities; second, predicting MGMT methylation status using a
convolutional neural network enhanced by adaptive sparse penalties. The
adaptive sparse penalty dynamically adjusts to variations in the data, such as
contrast differences and tumor locations in MR images. Our method excels in MRI
image synthesis, preserving brain tissue, fat, and individual tumor structures
across all MRI modalities. Validated on benchmark datasets, CAMP achieved an
accuracy of 0.97, specificity of 0.98, and sensitivity of 0.97, significantly
outperforming existing methods. These results demonstrate the potential of the
CAMP framework to improve the interpretation of MRI data and contribute to more
personalized treatment strategies for glioblastoma patients.

### [190] [Disentangled Multi-modal Learning of Histology and Transcriptomics for Cancer Characterization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16479)
*Yupei Zhang,Xiaofei Wang,Anran Liu,Lequan Yu,Chao Li*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种解耦多模态框架，结合组织病理学和转录组学，通过解决多模态异质性、多尺度整合、配对数据依赖和推理效率问题，在癌症诊断、预后和生存预测任务上超越了现有先进方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组织病理学是癌症诊断的金标准，结合转录组学可提供更全面的信息。然而，现有方法面临多模态异质性、多尺度整合不足以及对配对数据的依赖等挑战，限制了其临床应用。

Method: 本文提出了一个解耦多模态框架，包括四项主要贡献：1) 使用解耦多模态融合模块和置信度引导梯度协调策略，将WSIs和转录组分解为肿瘤和微环境子空间，以缓解多模态异质性。2) 提出跨放大倍数基因表达一致性策略，对齐WSI放大倍数间的转录组信号，以增强多尺度整合。3) 提出子空间知识蒸馏策略，通过仅WSI的学生模型实现转录组无关的推理，以减少对配对数据的依赖。4) 提出信息性Token聚合模块，在保留子空间语义的同时抑制WSI冗余，以提高推理效率。

Result: 在癌症诊断、预后和生存预测的广泛实验中，该框架在多种设置下均优于现有最先进的方法。

Conclusion: 所提出的解耦多模态框架有效解决了多模态异质性、多尺度整合不足和配对数据依赖等挑战，并在癌症相关任务中展现出卓越性能，提高了推理效率和临床适用性。

Abstract: Histopathology remains the gold standard for cancer diagnosis and prognosis.
With the advent of transcriptome profiling, multi-modal learning combining
transcriptomics with histology offers more comprehensive information. However,
existing multi-modal approaches are challenged by intrinsic multi-modal
heterogeneity, insufficient multi-scale integration, and reliance on paired
data, restricting clinical applicability. To address these challenges, we
propose a disentangled multi-modal framework with four contributions: 1) To
mitigate multi-modal heterogeneity, we decompose WSIs and transcriptomes into
tumor and microenvironment subspaces using a disentangled multi-modal fusion
module, and introduce a confidence-guided gradient coordination strategy to
balance subspace optimization. 2) To enhance multi-scale integration, we
propose an inter-magnification gene-expression consistency strategy that aligns
transcriptomic signals across WSI magnifications. 3) To reduce dependency on
paired data, we propose a subspace knowledge distillation strategy enabling
transcriptome-agnostic inference through a WSI-only student model. 4) To
improve inference efficiency, we propose an informative token aggregation
module that suppresses WSI redundancy while preserving subspace semantics.
Extensive experiments on cancer diagnosis, prognosis, and survival prediction
demonstrate our superiority over state-of-the-art methods across multiple
settings. Code is available at
https://github.com/helenypzhang/Disentangled-Multimodal-Learning.

### [191] [Time-Aware One Step Diffusion Network for Real-World Image Super-Resolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16557)
*Tainyi Zhang,Zheng-Peng Duan,Peng-Tao Jiang,Bo Li,Ming-Ming Cheng,Chun-Le Guo,Chongyi Li*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 针对基于扩散模型的单步真实世界图像超分辨率（Real-ISR）方法中固定时间步长无法充分利用预训练稳定扩散（SD）模型生成先验的问题，本文提出了TADSR，通过引入时间感知VAE编码器和时间感知VSD损失，实现了更有效的时间步长与潜在特征动态联合变化，从而在单步内达到最先进的性能和可控的超分辨率结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于变分分数蒸馏（VSD）的单步真实世界图像超分辨率（Real-ISR）方法，由于采用固定的时间步长来蒸馏预训练的稳定扩散（SD）模型，难以充分利用SD模型在不同噪声注入时间步长下表现出的不同生成先验，导致性能欠佳。

Method: 本文提出了一种时间感知单步扩散网络（TADSR）。具体方法包括：1) 引入一个时间感知VAE编码器，该编码器能根据不同的时间步长将同一图像投影到不同的潜在特征空间。2) 通过时间步长和潜在特征的动态联合变化，使学生模型更好地与预训练SD模型的输入模式分布对齐。3) 提出一种时间感知VSD损失，用于连接学生模型和教师模型的时间步长，从而在时间步长条件下产生更一致的生成先验指导。4) 利用SD在不同时间步长的生成先验，自然地实现了保真度和真实感之间可控的权衡。

Result: 实验结果表明，本文提出的方法在仅需一步的情况下，不仅实现了最先进的性能，而且能够生成可控的超分辨率结果。

Conclusion: TADSR通过其时间感知的设计（时间感知VAE编码器和时间感知VSD损失），成功解决了单步扩散模型Real-ISR中固定时间步长利用生成先验不足的问题，从而显著提升了性能，并提供了对超分辨率结果保真度和真实感的可控性。

Abstract: Diffusion-based real-world image super-resolution (Real-ISR) methods have
demonstrated impressive performance. To achieve efficient Real-ISR, many works
employ Variational Score Distillation (VSD) to distill pre-trained
stable-diffusion (SD) model for one-step SR with a fixed timestep. However, due
to the different noise injection timesteps, the SD will perform different
generative priors. Therefore, a fixed timestep is difficult for these methods
to fully leverage the generative priors in SD, leading to suboptimal
performance. To address this, we propose a Time-Aware one-step Diffusion
Network for Real-ISR (TADSR). We first introduce a Time-Aware VAE Encoder,
which projects the same image into different latent features based on
timesteps. Through joint dynamic variation of timesteps and latent features,
the student model can better align with the input pattern distribution of the
pre-trained SD, thereby enabling more effective utilization of SD's generative
capabilities. To better activate the generative prior of SD at different
timesteps, we propose a Time-Aware VSD loss that bridges the timesteps of the
student model and those of the teacher model, thereby producing more consistent
generative prior guidance conditioned on timesteps. Additionally, though
utilizing the generative prior in SD at different timesteps, our method can
naturally achieve controllable trade-offs between fidelity and realism by
changing the timestep condition. Experimental results demonstrate that our
method achieves both state-of-the-art performance and controllable SR results
with only a single step.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的3D LUT图像增强方法因缺乏空间信息而受限。虽然现有的空间感知3D LUT方法解决了这个问题，但它们引入了大量参数，并随着图像分辨率的增加导致运行时间显著增加。

Method: 该方法通过关注查找表的冗余部分来生成图像自适应LUT。其高效框架将一个3D LUT分解为低维LUT的线性总和，并利用奇异值分解（SVD）。此外，作者还优化了空间特征融合模块，使其更具缓存效率。

Result: 广泛的实验结果表明，该模型在保持空间感知和性能的同时，有效减少了参数数量和运行时间。

Conclusion: 通过分解3D LUT并优化空间特征融合，本文成功开发了一种高效、空间感知的图像增强方法，解决了现有3D LUT方法的局限性。

Abstract: The image enhancement methods based on 3D lookup tables (3D LUTs) efficiently
reduce both model size and runtime by interpolating pre-calculated values at
the vertices. However, the 3D LUT methods have a limitation due to their lack
of spatial information, as they convert color values on a point-by-point basis.
Although spatial-aware 3D LUT methods address this limitation, they introduce
additional modules that require a substantial number of parameters, leading to
increased runtime as image resolution increases. To address this issue, we
propose a method for generating image-adaptive LUTs by focusing on the
redundant parts of the tables. Our efficient framework decomposes a 3D LUT into
a linear sum of low-dimensional LUTs and employs singular value decomposition
(SVD). Furthermore, we enhance the modules for spatial feature fusion to be
more cache-efficient. Extensive experimental results demonstrate that our model
effectively decreases both the number of parameters and runtime while
maintaining spatial awareness and performance.

</details>


### [197] [Self-Validated Learning for Particle Separation: A Correctness-Based Self-Training Framework Without Human Labels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16224)
*Philipp D. Lösel,Aleese Barron,Yulai Zhang,Matthias Fabian,Benjamin Young,Nicolas Francois,Andrew M. Kingston*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为“自验证学习”的新型自训练框架，用于对大型多颗粒样本进行非破坏性3D实例分割，无需手动标注，通过迭代细化和自验证机制实现了高精度和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对大型多颗粒样本进行非破坏性3D成像对于量化颗粒特性至关重要，但在层析数据中准确分割颗粒面临形态变异大和颗粒接触频繁的挑战。传统方法如分水岭算法效果有限，而监督式深度学习虽性能更优，却依赖于耗时、易错且难以扩展的大规模标注数据集。

Method: 该方法提出“自验证学习”，这是一个无需手动标注的自训练框架。它利用隐式边界检测，并通过识别在同一样本的不同重排扫描中能一致匹配的颗粒，迭代地细化训练集。这种自验证机制减轻了噪声伪标签的影响，从而实现了从无标签数据中进行鲁棒学习。

Result: 经过三次迭代后，该方法在石英碎片的层析扫描中准确分割了超过97%的总颗粒体积，并识别出54,000多个单独颗粒。此外，该框架无需真实标签即可实现模型的完全自主评估，并已通过与最先进的实例分割技术比较得到证实。该方法已集成到Biomedisa图像分析平台中。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种无需手动标注的鲁棒自训练框架，能够准确、自主地对3D层析数据中的多颗粒样本进行实例分割，有效解决了传统方法和监督深度学习的局限性，并实现了高精度的分割性能和模型评估能力。

Abstract: Non-destructive 3D imaging of large multi-particulate samples is essential
for quantifying particle-level properties, such as size, shape, and spatial
distribution, across applications in mining, materials science, and geology.
However, accurate instance segmentation of particles in tomographic data
remains challenging due to high morphological variability and frequent particle
contact, which limit the effectiveness of classical methods like watershed
algorithms. While supervised deep learning approaches offer improved
performance, they rely on extensive annotated datasets that are
labor-intensive, error-prone, and difficult to scale. In this work, we propose
self-validated learning, a novel self-training framework for particle instance
segmentation that eliminates the need for manual annotations. Our method
leverages implicit boundary detection and iteratively refines the training set
by identifying particles that can be consistently matched across reshuffled
scans of the same sample. This self-validation mechanism mitigates the impact
of noisy pseudo-labels, enabling robust learning from unlabeled data. After
just three iterations, our approach accurately segments over 97% of the total
particle volume and identifies more than 54,000 individual particles in
tomographic scans of quartz fragments. Importantly, the framework also enables
fully autonomous model evaluation without the need for ground truth
annotations, as confirmed through comparisons with state-of-the-art instance
segmentation techniques. The method is integrated into the Biomedisa image
analysis platform (https://github.com/biomedisa/biomedisa/).

</details>


### [198] [Towards Diagnostic Quality Flat-Panel Detector CT Imaging Using Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16252)
*Hélène Corbaz,Anh Nguyen,Victor Schulze-Zachau,Paul Friedrich,Alicia Durrer,Florentin Bieder,Philippe C. Cattin,Marios N Psychogios*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本研究提出使用去噪扩散概率模型（DDPM）来提升介入手术室平板探测器CT（FDCT）的图像质量，使其可与多探测器CT（MDCT）媲美，以优化患者管理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 介入手术患者通常需要在术前和术后进行MDCT扫描，但将患者从介入室转移到MDCT室会增加管理复杂性。虽然介入室内的FDCT可以避免患者移动，但其图像质量远低于MDCT，存在显著伪影。因此，研究旨在提升FDCT图像质量，使其能够单独用于诊断，从而节省时间并改善患者管理。

Method: 本研究采用去噪扩散概率模型（DDPM）来改善FDCT扫描的图像质量。随后，临床医生通过问卷评估了原始FDCT、MDCT以及模型处理后的FDCT图像的诊断价值。

Result: DDPM模型成功消除了FDCT图像中的大部分伪影，显著提高了解剖结构的可视性，并且在不降低出血检测能力的前提下，使图像质量接近MDCT水平，前提是输入的FDCT图像质量不至于过低。

Conclusion: 去噪扩散概率模型（DDPM）能够有效提升FDCT图像质量，使其可用于诊断目的，从而有可能替代MDCT，简化介入手术患者的流程管理。

Abstract: Patients undergoing a mechanical thrombectomy procedure usually have a
multi-detector CT (MDCT) scan before and after the intervention. The image
quality of the flat panel detector CT (FDCT) present in the intervention room
is generally much lower than that of a MDCT due to significant artifacts.
However, using only FDCT images could improve patient management as the patient
would not need to be moved to the MDCT room. Several studies have evaluated the
potential use of FDCT imaging alone and the time that could be saved by
acquiring the images before and/or after the intervention only with the FDCT.
This study proposes using a denoising diffusion probabilistic model (DDPM) to
improve the image quality of FDCT scans, making them comparable to MDCT scans.
Clinicans evaluated FDCT, MDCT, and our model's predictions for diagnostic
purposes using a questionnaire. The DDPM eliminated most artifacts and improved
anatomical visibility without reducing bleeding detection, provided that the
input FDCT image quality is not too low. Our code can be found on github.

</details>

### [199] [NeuroKoop: Neural Koopman Fusion of Structural-Functional Connectomes for Identifying Prenatal Drug Exposure in Adolescents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16414)
*Badhan Mazumder,Aline Kotoski,Vince D. Calhoun,Dong Hye Ye*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文提出NeuroKoop，一种基于图神经网络的框架，利用Koopman算子驱动的潜在空间融合，整合结构和功能脑网络，以更准确地分类产前药物暴露（PDE）状态并揭示其对青少年大脑组织的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解产前暴露于大麻等精神活性物质如何影响青少年大脑组织是一个重大挑战，现有分析方法难以充分捕捉结构和功能连接组中的互补特征，限制了生物学洞察力和预测性能。

Method: 引入了NeuroKoop，一种新型的基于图神经网络的框架。该框架利用神经Koopman算子驱动的潜在空间融合技术，整合了源基形态学（SBM）和功能网络连接（FNC）生成的脑图谱，从而统一节点嵌入，增强表征学习。

Result: 将NeuroKoop应用于ABCD数据集中的大型青少年队列，其性能优于相关基线方法，并揭示了显著的结构-功能连接，加深了对产前药物暴露神经发育影响的理解。

Conclusion: NeuroKoop通过整合多模态脑网络数据，提高了产前药物暴露状态的分类准确性，并为理解其神经发育影响提供了新的生物学洞察。

Abstract: Understanding how prenatal exposure to psychoactive substances such as
cannabis shapes adolescent brain organization remains a critical challenge,
complicated by the complexity of multimodal neuroimaging data and the
limitations of conventional analytic methods. Existing approaches often fail to
fully capture the complementary features embedded within structural and
functional connectomes, constraining both biological insight and predictive
performance. To address this, we introduced NeuroKoop, a novel graph neural
network-based framework that integrates structural and functional brain
networks utilizing neural Koopman operator-driven latent space fusion. By
leveraging Koopman theory, NeuroKoop unifies node embeddings derived from
source-based morphometry (SBM) and functional network connectivity (FNC) based
brain graphs, resulting in enhanced representation learning and more robust
classification of prenatal drug exposure (PDE) status. Applied to a large
adolescent cohort from the ABCD dataset, NeuroKoop outperformed relevant
baselines and revealed salient structural-functional connections, advancing our
understanding of the neurodevelopmental impact of PDE.

</details>
